<div id="review_306482312" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/306482312" />
    <a title="Heidi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5893535-heidi"><img alt="Heidi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581863475p2/5893535.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/306482312?book_show_action=true">Apr 04, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heidi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heidi" href="/user/show/5893535-heidi">Heidi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780575082373" href="/book/show/2016634.House_of_Suns">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">fans of epic space opera and characters with depth</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5893535-heidi?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5893535-heidi?shelf=format-paper">format-paper</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5893535-heidi?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5893535-heidi?shelf=sf-space-opera">sf-space-opera</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5893535-heidi?shelf=winners-sci-fi">winners-sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5893535-heidi?shelf=author-reynolds">author-reynolds</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5893535-heidi?shelf=sf-ai-and-robots">sf-ai-and-robots</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5893535-heidi?shelf=me-heartbreaker">me-heartbreaker</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer306482312" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7031309637147706716">If it was possible to give this novel 6 stars, I would. I finished it just half an hour ago, and I'm still floating out there in space, unwilling to return to the confinements of our small blue planet.<br/><br/>"House of Suns" is big in every sense of the word, and it would have been easy to bury the characters, their feelings and relationships under the vast scope of time the story covers, the gigantic spaceships, the huge mysteries and conflicts. <br/>That doesn't happen. Amidst the rise and fall of entire c</span>
  <span id="freeText7031309637147706716" style="display:none">If it was possible to give this novel 6 stars, I would. I finished it just half an hour ago, and I'm still floating out there in space, unwilling to return to the confinements of our small blue planet.<br /><br />"House of Suns" is big in every sense of the word, and it would have been easy to bury the characters, their feelings and relationships under the vast scope of time the story covers, the gigantic spaceships, the huge mysteries and conflicts. <br />That doesn't happen. Amidst the rise and fall of entire civilisations, the destiny of Purslane and Campion, essentially two clones of a young woman named Abigail Gentian, but also fully fledged individuals with their own histories and personalities, and the golden robot Hesperus rises to a grandeur of its own.<br /><br />There are no aliens in this novel, but over the course of millions of years, humanity has evolved into many different forms of sentient life, many of which are barely recognisable as humans anymore.<br />Abigail's clones are - though augmented - human through and through, in every respect, and they have all their creator's memories of a time when humanity was still confined to our solar system. But what happens if you combine almost godlike powers and a life span bordering on immortality with human fallibility and instable character traits? <br /><br />I'm sure even this book has its flaws, and if I take it apart, I might find them. But I don't want to. I enjoyed every single page, the tight and fast-paced storytelling, the characterisations, the mysteries piled up on top of other mysteries and the fact that, with few lesser important exceptions, the author resolves all of them. There are no significant loose threads left in the end. <br />The science aspects partly went straight over my head, but I don't have to understand <i>how</i> something works, but what it <i>does</i>, and Reynolds served my needs just fine.<br /><br />"House of Suns" is definitely an all-time favourite, and for once I cherish the fact that I tend to forget things pretty quickly. When I pick it up again in a few years, it might just feel like the first time, and that's surely something to look forward to.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7031309637147706716" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2008450864?book_show_action=true">May 23, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jamie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jamie" href="/user/show/53587416-jamie">Jamie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/53587416-jamie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2008450864" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9034590836041141926">Mind blowing, intergalactic awesomeness on an immense scale. This is a story of brewing conflict between human civilization of the far future and the rise of robot/machine sentient civilization. And all wrapped up in a (mass) murder mystery. I could not ask for anything more from my sci-fi. I was already an <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/51204.Alastair_Reynolds' title='Alastair Reynolds' rel='nofollow noopener'>Alastair Reynolds</a> fan after reading <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/89187.Revelation_Space' title='Revelation Space by Alastair Reynolds' rel='nofollow noopener'>Revelation Space</a>, but this seals the deal.</span>
  <span id="freeText9034590836041141926" style="display:none">Mind blowing, intergalactic awesomeness on an immense scale. This is a story of brewing conflict between human civilization of the far future and the rise of robot/machine sentient civilization. And all wrapped up in a (mass) murder mystery. I could not ask for anything more from my sci-fi. I was already an <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/51204.Alastair_Reynolds" title="Alastair Reynolds" rel="nofollow noopener">Alastair Reynolds</a> fan after reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/89187.Revelation_Space" title="Revelation Space by Alastair Reynolds" rel="nofollow noopener">Revelation Space</a>, but this seals the deal.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ct7rWm/B56+fmRMU84m6EpbZDDv+9/oM4o1GjF3bnZZwj9WN0Sd4sCDsmJE7MEhBql+vOvym5RhTJ51RcD4KZQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('5Y+Hn3xt75fgJ8BTWgqNfirEb+ttDnPBwjfvG9/06x/n3rlIwotwiF9SS9aSs38tFkLM6m9fbNVznTTG8hF87A==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer13791933563986636125">I'm Al, now a Goodreads author. I used to be a space scientist, and now I'm a writer, although for a time the two careers ran in parallel. I started off publishing short stories in the British SF magazine Interzone in the early 90s, then eventually branched into novels. I write about a novel a year and try to write a few short stories as well. Some of my books and stories are set in a consistent f</span>
  <span id="freeText13791933563986636125" style="display:none">I'm Al, now a Goodreads author. I used to be a space scientist, and now I'm a writer, although for a time the two careers ran in parallel. I started off publishing short stories in the British SF magazine Interzone in the early 90s, then eventually branched into novels. I write about a novel a year and try to write a few short stories as well. Some of my books and stories are set in a consistent future named after Revelation Space, the first novel, but I've done a lot of other things as well and I like to keep things fresh between books. <br /><br />I was born in Wales, but raised in Cornwall, and then spent time in the north of England and Scotland. I moved to the Netherlands to continue my science career and stayed there for a very long time, before eventually returning to Wales.<br /><br />In my spare time I am a very keen runner, and I also enjoying hill-walking, birdwatching, horse-riding, guitar and model-making. I also dabble with paints now and then. I met my wife in the Netherlands through a mutual interest in climbing and we married back in Wales. We live surrounded by hills, woods and wildlife, and not too much excitement.</span>
